commit ad2633bbe12cf35eb9da7cfc0b63759542c1dd83
Author: yarukishi <150128243+yarukishi@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Sat Oct 12 23:45:14 2024 +0900

    Scale surveyors and gun emplacements for high population (#1102)
    
    When the high population trait is in effect, gun emplacements now reduce the number of soldiers required to guard the soul forge by a scaled value. This addresses #1094.
    
    This change also adds high population scaling to Hell Surveyors in the following ways:
    - Job count and maximum carport damage scaling based on high population value (usually 4x)
    - Carport repair scaling based on growth value (usually 3.5x)
    - Surveyor danger scaling based on high population value (usually 4x)
    - Infernite output is worker scaled (usually 0.26x) for high population
    - Maximum demon bodies searched for soul gems by each surveyor are worker scaled down from 100 bodies (usually to 26 bodies)
    
    Separately, the method of distributing predator drone kills to surveyors is slightly modified for improved accuracy.
    
    This change will vastly increase surveyor deaths for insectoid races, so it's recommended to merge this together with or after PR #1082. I tested all of the changes, and each change appears to work as expected.
    
    Co-authored-by: Peter Motschmann <pmotsch3@gmail.com>

commit f9e4e243b0b71d16048134963fcc4e2039c4e076
Author: yarukishi <150128243+yarukishi@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Thu Sep 26 13:16:03 2024 +0900

    Fix scientific notation; use locale number formats (#1208)
    
    * Fix scientific notation; use locale number formats
    
    Evolve's default number display mode, SI, is actually engineering notation, because it uses only exponents that are multiples of 3. In addition, it can't handle exponents larger than 27.
    
    Fix these deficiencies:
    - Change scientific notation to use any integer exponent.
    - Create a new engineering notation selection for users who like the current behavior.
    
    For quite large numbers (1e27 and larger), metric suffixes become inadequate.
    - Numbers 1e27 or larger use SI instead of a suffix.
    
    Locale-aware number formatting is available in Hell observation statistics, but absent in the rest of the game. This is a good opportunity to provide locale-aware number formatting to more places.
    - Use locale-aware formatting in sizeApproximation()
    - Change "fixed" (always 1 fractional digit) to "precise", which enforces a minimum precision and displays at least all integer digits. This mode is used for Hell observations.
    - Add new "exact" parameter that forces all fractional digits to display, even if the number gets really big. This is used for prestige resource counts.
    
    * Allow +1 sigfig for single leading digit
    
    Displayed number of digits is the same for leading zero and leading nonzero, even though apparent significant figure count is different
    
    * More accurate comment
    
    * Fix force SI logic to really be SI (not Eng)

    Devilish dish expansion (#1200)
    
    Changed up how the devilish dish works.
    Devilish Dish, Life Infuser and Soul steeper no longer unlocked all at once after codex infinium.
    Devilish dish tech now available after codex infernium, it's now a stepping stone for the next tech.
    Soul-Vide Cooker (tech) becomes available after devilish dish tech and hell lake analysis. It unlocks a new segmented structure.
    Soul-Vide Cooker (building) when complete, can be enabled to start creation of the devilish dish. Without any aid, it takes 100000 days to complete.
    After codex infinium and once the dish reaches 0.05% done (50 days), a new tech called "preparation methods" is unlocked which unlocks the soul steeper and life infuser to speed up the creation of the dish.
    
    Soul steeper now grants +5% speed per spire floor cleared per steeper and is no longer compounding and no longer required to create the dish at all.
    Life infuser costs population to create and grants +15% speed
    
    Misc changes:
    Fixed fasting chthonian piracy objective to only require 0 chthonian piracy (for real this time)
    Added wiki stuff for new buildings.
    Fixed missing string for banquet hall on wiki

commit b8e77b6e22d6379e32fed2ddcee4aed9c72e6ca3
Author: yarukishi <150128243+yarukishi@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Mon Sep 2 09:12:59 2024 +0900

    Fix support calculation for gateway and remove fractional ships (#1174)
    
    The support calculation for Andromeda ships in the Gateway system incorrectly provided too much support in cases when the lowest-priority ship receiving support was a Frigate, Cruiser, or Dreadnought.
    
    For example, suppose that the Gateway System has 32.5 support and the following ships activated:
    31 Bolognium Ship > 6 Dreadnought > 5 Cruiser Ship > 2 Frigate Ship
    
    In this situation, we expect 31 Bolognium Ships (31 support), 0.3 Dreadnoughts (1.5 support), 0 Cruiser Ships, and 0 Frigate Ships to operate.
    
    Actually, the game operates 31 Bolognium Ships (correct), 1.5 Dreadnoughts (too many), 0 Cruiser Ships, and 2 Frigate Ships. This is a total of 31 + 7.5 + 4 = 42.5 Gateway support. It prints that only 24.5 / 32.50 support is in use.
    
    Fixing this issue causes some ugly rounding problems with fractional ships, especially in relationship to Cruiser Ships (3 support) that are being moved around. I chose to remove fractional ship support as part of the patch.
    
    If we want to keep fractional ships, then fixing all of the rounding issues is probably feasible.

commit f2b3f36e995ee3aa87c12c93577ff5366b3a61d2
Author: yarukishi <150128243+yarukishi@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Tue Aug 6 13:23:27 2024 +0900

    Improve tab refresh behavior (#1125)
    
    * Improve tab refresh behavior
    
    The code to refresh governor actions generally assumes that it is being executed on the tab where the action is made visible. However, Evolve has building and research queues, so these triggers might happen while the GUI is viewing any tab. Update the restrictions so that governor tasks are immediately refreshed even without Preload Tab Content enabled.
    
    The defineGovernor() function now accordingly checks for its own visibility before it redraws the GUI.
    
    Some completely missing governor tab refreshes, such as when adding or removing Slavery or Cannibalism, or when researching certain technologies, have also been added.
    
    Additionally, remove various instances where the resource panel was deleted and redrawn, which seems to be legacy that isn't required anymore. The simple action of unlocking crates / containers is good enough to make those resources visible, to add the + buttons for per-resource storage management, and for the associated storage type to appear within the modal.
    
    Containers may be unlocked by any building that grants them, because, unlike crates, containers aren't mandatory to progress in the game. Add a variety of checks for this, so even a user whose first container is provided by a building other than the container port or wharf can get the proper unlocks.
    
    * Fix tab condition check when learning Personal Assistant

    Screen reader: make more menus usable (#1111)
    
    The Truepath ship constructor, mech constructor and industry tab > matter replicater menus all have to be hovered on with the mouse in order to open them.     commit 582b20fcfb6ce74e0a6d8a8c5f6e7922a539348c
    Author: yarukishi <150128243+yarukishi@users.noreply.github.com>
    Date:   Fri Feb 16 02:13:11 2024 +0900
    
        Prevent exploits to assign too many crafters
    
        Scarletite and Quantium limit the number of craftsmen working on them
        based on the number of associated buildings that are currently
        operating. Scarletite crafters are intended to be removed when an
        Infernal Forge is powered off, but if the game is paused, then they can
        be reassigned before the crafting window is reloaded. Also, crafters may
        be assigned even when the forge is not
        receiving enough power. Quantium
        crafters are never forcibly removed
        when a lab is powered down.
    
        This change introduces a check for job limits on specific types of
        craftsmen. It directly precedes the overall job limit, which can remove
        only craftsmen that exceed the overall craftsman limit.

    commit 149bc933dc30acaba48f23341ce98acc84d9cf53
    Author: yarukishi <150128243+yarukishi@users.noreply.github.com>
    Date:   Fri Feb 16 22:55:21 2024 +0900
    
        Add missing save file upgrade logic (#1072)
    
        * Add missing save upgrade logic that was lost in commit 28b4e46
    
        A commit in version 1.3.0 beta 8 simplified the initialization routines
        for various structures to use loops. These loops set all values to 0 or
        false. However, custom save upgrade logic existed for two values, and
        this logic was lost in the transition.
    
        1. In 0.9.0, the showCiv property was created. It was seeded with
           the value of showCity for old saves. Currently, loading a save from
           prior to 0.9.0 will unconditionally set showCiv to false, so post-
           sentience saves will fail to show the main tab and cannot naturally
           recover without a soft reset, a prestige reset, or save file editing.
    
        2. In approximately 0.4.9 / 0.4.10, the counter for demonic invasions
           was created. Older save files that have the Doomed achievement
           initialized this counter to 1, so restore this logic as well.
    
        * Fix default locale for save file upgrades from en-us to en-US

    commit e5d6c079fefb0aacf24be66718fc79b12a65cc2a
    Author: yarukishi <150128243+yarukishi@users.noreply.github.com>
    Date:   Thu Feb 15 14:08:05 2024 +0900
    
        Convert slaves into a normal resource (#1012)
    
        Currently, slaves are stored as a count on the slave pen structure, and they are mirrored as a global resource for display purposes. This causes a value mismatch when a tax riot occurs, where slaves appear to be killed but are not. Change all references to the slave pen version of slave count into the global resource version.
    
    commit 8d9abcf079ebdcdc1567af764e061aae3fbf5724
    Author: yarukishi <150128243+yarukishi@users.noreply.github.com>
    Date:   Thu Feb 15 14:06:29 2024 +0900
    
        Fix priority inversion of DNA sequencer and build queues (#1023)
    
        The conditions for the DNA sequencer and the build/research queues to consume the Knowledge resource are different. As a result, structs and techs that require Knowledge may never build when automatic sequencing is enabled. Specifically, this may occur when Knowledge production less than 10k per day.
    
        To allow queues to function for structs and techs near the Knowledge cap at that time, set the DNA sequencer buffer size to the lesser of 10,000 and the Knowledge production value.
    
        Fixes issues #322 and #672.

commit d13c00c6621602e580af5a18cfcc77558cdd47e3
Author: yarukishi <150128243+yarukishi@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Fri Feb 16 03:59:22 2024 +0900

    Fix missing UI refresh for crafter count

commit 582b20fcfb6ce74e0a6d8a8c5f6e7922a539348c
Author: yarukishi <150128243+yarukishi@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Fri Feb 16 02:13:11 2024 +0900

    Prevent exploits to assign too many crafters
    
    Scarletite and Quantium limit the number of craftsmen working on them
    based on the number of associated buildings that are currently
    operating. Scarletite crafters are intended to be removed when an
    Infernal Forge is powered off, but if the game is paused, then they can
    be reassigned before the crafting window is reloaded. Also, crafters may
    be assigned even when the forge is not
    receiving enough power. Quantium
    crafters are never forcibly removed
    when a lab is powered down.
    
    This change introduces a check for job limits on specific types of
    craftsmen. It directly precedes the overall job limit, which can remove
    only craftsmen that exceed the overall craftsman limit.

commit 149bc933dc30acaba48f23341ce98acc84d9cf53
Author: yarukishi <150128243+yarukishi@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Fri Feb 16 22:55:21 2024 +0900

    Add missing save file upgrade logic (#1072)
    
    * Add missing save upgrade logic that was lost in commit 28b4e46
    
    A commit in version 1.3.0 beta 8 simplified the initialization routines
    for various structures to use loops. These loops set all values to 0 or
    false. However, custom save upgrade logic existed for two values, and
    this logic was lost in the transition.
    
    1. In 0.9.0, the showCiv property was created. It was seeded with
       the value of showCity for old saves. Currently, loading a save from
       prior to 0.9.0 will unconditionally set showCiv to false, so post-
       sentience saves will fail to show the main tab and cannot naturally
       recover without a soft reset, a prestige reset, or save file editing.
    
    2. In approximately 0.4.9 / 0.4.10, the counter for demonic invasions
       was created. Older save files that have the Doomed achievement
       initialized this counter to 1, so restore this logic as well.
    
    * Fix default locale for save file upgrades from en-us to en-US

commit 8b49e5954eec85c1dd813b7a341a24f28d19a6ea
Author: yarukishi <150128243+yarukishi@users.noreply.github.com>

    Add setting to auto-power all new structs (#1010)
    
    * Fix return status of powerOnNewStruct
    
    Move "return true" inside of the check for power. Also, update the current available power status even when matter replicator governor task is off, so that future invocations are also correct.
    
    * Always set powered() to electricity cost

    - Add support() function to the zoo
    - Check for available support before enabling Tau Ceti mining ships and whaling ships

commit e5d6c079fefb0aacf24be66718fc79b12a65cc2a
Author: yarukishi <150128243+yarukishi@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Thu Feb 15 14:08:05 2024 +0900

    Convert slaves into a normal resource (#1012)
    
    Currently, slaves are stored as a count on the slave pen structure, and they are mirrored as a global resource for display purposes. This causes a value mismatch when a tax riot occurs, where slaves appear to be killed but are not. Change all references to the slave pen version of slave count into the global resource version.

commit 8d9abcf079ebdcdc1567af764e061aae3fbf5724
Author: yarukishi <150128243+yarukishi@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Thu Feb 15 14:06:29 2024 +0900

    Fix priority inversion of DNA sequencer and build queues (#1023)
    
    The conditions for the DNA sequencer and the build/research queues to consume the Knowledge resource are different. As a result, structs and techs that require Knowledge may never build when automatic sequencing is enabled. Specifically, this may occur when Knowledge production less than 10k per day.
    
    To allow queues to function for structs and techs near the Knowledge cap at that time, set the DNA sequencer buffer size to the lesser of 10,000 and the Knowledge production value.
    
    Fixes issues #322 and #672.

Author: yarukishi <150128243+yarukishi@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Wed Dec 6 22:45:09 2023 +0900

    Allow all non-Micro universes to improve Evolve Adept perk
    
    The Evolve Novice through Grandmaster feats all depend on the achievement level of some number of achievements, as well as the highest completed challenge level of the matching reset tier. Unlike all of the other reset tiers, Black Hole / Vacuum Collapse resets have unique achievements for each universe, so the White Hole achievement level in the Standard universe cannot increase as a result of resets in non-Standard, non-Micro universes.
    
    Change the perk effect of Evolve Adept to consider the black hole / vacuum collapse achievements from the Evil, Antimatter, Heavy, and Magic universes on equal standing to White Hole. Micro is excluded.

commit 64fc33f6f87a6e4e4334f2eab163f3cd2ff9193c
Author: yarukishi <150128243+yarukishi@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Wed Nov 15 11:04:58 2023 +0900

    Add biome restrictions to cold snap and heat wave (#990)
    
    Certain biomes enforce temperature characteristics, so this seems like an oversight.
    
    Volcanic and ashland biomes are "always hot" in the summer, so prevent cold snap at that time. Tundra and taiga biomes are the opposite, "always cold" in the winter, so prevent heat wave at that time.
    
    Hellscape is "never cold," so prevent the cold snap event with no regard to the current season. Allow the event on a Permafrost Hellscape (custom) planet as an exception.
    
    Eden is idyllic, so it normally can be hot only in summer (typically non-winter) and cold only in winter (typically non-summer). To preserve a one-step improvement in seasonal temperature range versus standard temperature biomes, prohibit cold snap in summer and heat wave in winter.
    
    Continue to allow winter heat waves and summer cold snaps for normal biomes.

commit ebb7ab3009f79a6885c1ce75d0fbdaa671228a79
Author: Beorseder <45007766+Beorseder@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Tue Aug 9 01:05:24 2022 -0600

    Misc Fixes
    
    Game:
    Fixed Hell Observation tab loading problem for preloaders without the observe object created yet.
    Fixed Genetics tech not working in Cataclysm.
    Made Revive's usage in Hell Dimension use Math.rand instead of seededRandom, to prevent the trait being used for the by far easiest method of advancing the seed. Use of the warseed to keep seededness did not seem warranted, as the mechanic is something that happens automatically everyday and thus not something people would care to try to reroll.
    
    Wiki:
    Added 1/8th second delay before page scrolling in the wiki happens to let the page elements load in before the scrolling position is calculated. This fixes the problem where the page would overscroll if it wasn't already open, scrolling increasingly too far the deeper down the page it needed to go.
    Fixed Industrialization, Planetary, and Space tabs in the wiki not fully loading in without a save.
    Removed Terraform button's # built input in the wiki.
    Added # inputs to Space Probe, G.E.C.K., and Bioseeder Ship wiki entries.
    Fixed Atmosphere Terraformer showing Ascension Machine effect when # built is 100 in the wiki.
    Updated Job Stress mechanics entry with High Pop.
    Updated prestige calculators to show Terraforming reset as a dropdown option and make the Truepath checkbox disabled if Cataclysm is selected.
    Updated Flare and Unstable planet entries to mention their unique events.
    Updated Seeded Randomness entry to be a little more accurate about resets.
    Updated a couple wiki entries to mention Sludge.
    Updated Religion mechanics entry to reflect new mechanic of Fanaticism ranking a trait up if it is already had and not max rank already.
    Updated Infiltrator trait wiki string to be more accurate about how it affects scouting.
    Updated Kroll/Cambridge process wiki entries to be accurate.
    Updated Exotic Infusion1&2 tech entries to say that they're confirmations and don't spend resources, to avoid confusion.
    
    Misc Strings:
    Updated Pig-Latin.
    Localized ARPA "Level - X" string.
    Updated Governor Theorist and Inspirational traits to say Cement worker instead of Factory worker (since everyone always thinks it's Factories).
    Updated Socialist and Corpocracy Governments to say that they affect factories and manufacturing plants, and updated their wiki entries to specifically state how they boost Cement Plant Workers and Graphene Plants in addition to Factories.

commit 5ba52b6ea0beba501266638cbeadc536d8e5fa0f
Author: Beorseder <45007766+Beorseder@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Mon Aug 8 07:14:43 2022 -0600

    Hell Observation Update
    
    Main Points:
    Added chart.js script to game.
    Added data and tracking of all events that occur in Hell Dimension each day through bloodwar().
    Added new hidden Hell Observations tab in which this data and tracking can be seen.
    
    Details:
    Hell Observations
     - This tab is in the same tier as Civilization, Civics, Research, etc., but is hidden by having it disabled and appear with no name. In the case that any additional non-hidden tabs get added to this tier in the future, they should be placed before it as there will otherwise be a gap. Accessing this tab already calculates the civTab number with the intention of it being the last in the list, so any future tabs added in-between shouldn't affect it.
     - This tab is accessed through clicking the new "Hell Observations" button located in the fortress, either in the Hell Dimension or Military tab.
     - The Hell Observations tab has two components: Report Logs and Analysis.
    
    Report Logs
     - All events that occur each day are compiled into a Report Log that can be accessed in the Report Logs subtab, showing in chronological order said reported events that day.
     - Because of the potentially very large size of these logs, they are not saved in any way and will disappear on refresh.
     - Furthermore, for the purposes of tab-loading, the recent at most 2500 logs will be kept. After passing 2500, a year of logs will be purged.
    
    Analysis
     - Each day, much of the data of what happened in Hell Dimension will be added to sum totals. These totals can be seen in the Analysis subtab. While report logs are not saved, this more condensed analytical data is kept in the save.
     - For the purposes of comparison or tracking the stats of a new hell configuration, data is added each day to two different datasets. One totals the entirety of Hell Dimension data for the run, and the second can be reset at any time to begin tracking totally new data.
     - Averages, conversion to various units of time, and adjustment for Hyper/Slow can be easily toggled to.
     - Graphs can be created to showcase data in a different manner. Currently only Pie graphs exist, though more types utilizing different data can be added later and had been planned.

commit b266505629146eab2fa0a9ebad32403358c92ce0
Author: Peter Motschmann <pmotsch3@gmail.com>
Date:   Fri Apr 1 09:45:46 2022 -0400

    1.2.14 patch notes

commit c04f669bc4a002f707c7b28547a2db0afdc35688
Author: Beorseder <45007766+Beorseder@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Fri Apr 1 05:48:49 2022 -0600

    Bugs and Wiki
    
    Game QoL:
    Added Titan Mine slider to Industry tab.
    Added additional popup confirmation to Restore Backup.
    The game now no longer automatically makes a backup when the webpage starts up if none exists, always normally resulting in a completely fresh save being backed up for no real reason.
    Nanite Factory interface now has tooltips for each resource that list conversion rates and how much is currently being consumed/produced.
    Nanite production tooltip now lists how much is coming from each resource, instead of saying nothing.
    Made ship destination tooltips in Shipyard align such that the scrollbars are no longer cut off.
    
    Misc:
    The Vault Discovery event can now no longer occur if there are 0 Archaeologists assigned and/or if Suppression is at 0%.
    Fixed problem with The Fool feat and the April Fool's achievements tab prank where it could only be gotten within the first day after refreshing the page if Preload Tab Content was disabled, making it difficult and inconsistent for many people to find.
    Fixed genome Deterioration messages displaying a time to reach genome decay that was off by a factor of (1+mutations) of the actual amount.
    Updated Mass Ejector assigning and Mass Ejector Optimizer Governor task to use p_on['mass_ejector'] instead of mass_ejector.on to be more accurate in the off-cases where some Mass Ejectors aren't getting enough power. This fixes the bug where one could infinitely raise ejection amounts when this was happening.
    Also in the case where this is happening, the Mass Ejector tab will say next to the max what the actual active max is to avoid confusion.
    Added a drawTech() after the AI Super Core finishes building. Fixes #738
    Updated Pig Latin.
    
    Wiki:
    Added each tech's tech tree and # in the tree to their wiki entries at top right like with CRISPR.
    Added Vault Discovery Progress Event entry to wiki.
    Added explanation for how Hazards are generated to wiki hazard entry.
    Made Doomed perk string and Regenerative trait effect string more clear. Also updated wiki planet entry to say that up to 2 extra traits can be gotten.
    Fixed VR Training wiki entry saying Hospital instead of Boot Camp.
    Made structure wiki entry creep calculations bottom out at 1.005.
    Added a "Time to 0.025 Exotic Solar Masses" calc to the Mass Mechanics entry calcs.
    Made Content input not show in Job Stress calc if Soldier or Hunter is selected.
    Fixed some prestige calculators not replacing words with values for AI Apocalypse reset selected and some incorrect calculations being shown.
    Fixed Quantum Mechanics entry saying Swarm Control AI instead of Quantum Computing in an instance.

commit 2cd5860161e23a0a160cd9c4be4876fbf98dbd6b
Author: Beorseder <45007766+Beorseder@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Tue Feb 15 22:05:21 2022 -0700

    Calculator Updates, Minor Bug Fixes, and Info
    
    Perks:
    Added Doomed achievement to the perks lists because there's no way to know that it unlocks Hellscape/Eden planets otherwise.
    Added Governor CRISPR tree to perks list.
    Fixed Evolve Journeyman not showing the full list of values in the wiki perks page if the perk was not yet obtained.
    
    Calculators:
    Updated Plasmid/Anti-Plasmid gain calculators with the new caps on gains, the High Population trait, being Synthetic genus for MADs, and being in Truepath, and AI Apocalypse reset.
    Updated Phage gain calculator with Truepath and AI Apocalypse reset.
    Updated Dark Energy bonus calculator with Lemon Cleaner perk.
    Added AI Core gain and bonus calculators.
    Added gain calculators to AI Apocalypse reset entry.
    Updated Job Stress calculator to be fixed and accommodate for trait rankings and, the Emotionless trait and to fix Titan Colonist string.
    
    Wiki Info:
    Added information about Sludge's modification costing 10x more and their inability to remove Ooze to the Failed Experiment entry. Also fixed the data link to MAD reset.
    Similarly added to CRISPR Mutation entry that Sludge also have 10x costs.
    Added to Raid, Siege, and Terrorist Attack events how they don't happen in Truepath.
    Added Pillage event(s) entry to Major Events page.
    Updated Llama Minor Event with trait restrictions.
    Updated Ascension reset entry with information on the geology buff and Ascended planets.
    Added wiki effect to Alien Biotech tech.
    
    Textual:
    Fixed Entertainer tooltip showing twice the effect of Musical.
    Fixed Gauss Rifles showing the effect for Disruptor Rifles.
    Fixed some wiki fuel cost displays.
    Fixed Water Freighter tooltip showing half the Helium-3 cost. Fixes #713
    Fixed some typos.
    Changed instances of "space cost creep" to "non-homeworld cost creep" to indicate that they apply to Hell Dimension as well.
    Updated Pig-Latin.
    
    Misc:
    Exporting the save now updates accelerated time bank to account for if someone is paused and exports, updating their save's current time and thus losing all that accelerated time.
    Fixed CRISPR and Blood Infusions being affected by adjustCosts when checking their affordability, which caused some issues with traits shifting their costs around making the coloring inaccurate sometimes near the cost.
    Fixed Ritual Casting not showing up in Industry in Cataclysm.
    Fixed bug where, if not Preloading Tab Content, shifting to another tab when in the custom lab and then shifting back to Civilization tab would not show the custom lab anymore. Fixes #671
    Detritivores no longer see the Farming ritual as it doesn't do anything for them.
    Fixed bug with building the Forward Base not reloading space to show the Troop Lander and Crashed Ship structures.

commit 2977f15aa9ace3b0f213c790d144479f556da5d7
Author: Beorseder <45007766+Beorseder@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Sun Oct 17 20:22:44 2021 -0600

    Queue Behavior Changes/Fixes + Build
    
    In ordered queues, Green Nevers (which happen when you have the potential cap for a resource, but don't have enough of it currently and don't have the production to ever produce it) now will not be barriers in the queue, freezing the queue on them and preventing the things after it from being completed. Now, they will act just like Red Nevers (which happen when you don't have the potential cap for a resource), and the queue will skip past them and move to the next item.
    
    Fixed bug where in unordered queues an ARPA project at the end of the queue with a Never completion would block the rest of the queue from being completed. Fixes #488 Fixes #613
    
    Fixed bug where the time estimations on buildings/techs could calculate an actual number as an estimate instead of Never when the building would in fact never complete. This was caused by the timeCheck functions proceeding to check the times for all the resources that something costs, even after it determines that it will never complete from one resource. So if any resource after that one that never completes does complete and was the determined bottleneck for that building/tech, then the -9999999 time was overridden by that bottleneck's time. Now if it determines that something will never complete, it skips past the remaining resources.
    
    Added Play/Pause buttons next to the building queue and research queue titles that let you pause and resume each the queues.
    
    Updated Queue Mechanics entry with info about queue merging options and pause/play.

Date:   Sat Aug 7 01:06:08 2021 -0600

    Queue QoL
    
    Added "Research Queue" title above the research queue.
    
    Added (Used/Max) section to Building Queue and Research Queue headings to indicate how many slots of each respective queue is being used and are currently possible. Looks like "Building Queue (10/20)".
    
    Added Queue Merging settings options. There are three options to accommodate various building queue merging options that people have requested. The first option never combines items in the building queue. The second option functions just as the queue does currently, combining nearby items of the same type. The third option will merge all items of the same time in the queue, regardless of position. Fixes #258  Fixes #497
    
    Fixed issue where queues could end up with having excess amounts of items in them when using a governor that expands the queue, queueing up items past the max one one would without that governor, and then unassigning that governor. In this situation, it will trim however many items from the end of the queue that are in excess.

    Truepath Rival

commit bfbb4cd6e6cfb275c08ddc9f9af01b28f9fea942
Author: Beorseder <45007766+Beorseder@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Mon Jun 14 05:24:42 2021 -0600

    String Packs
    
    Implemented the ability to import and use "String Packs". They're basically like resource packs in Minecraft. Just a way for people to customize the look of their game more, purely visual. It essentially allows for a locally sourced language file that sits on top of the language chosen, just as non-English languages sit on top of English, which serves as the basis. Wiki entry (Mechanics -> String Pack) explains in detail what one is and how one can be made.
    As a plus, it could be a good vehicle for promoting the game and bolstering the community, as I'm sure themed packs will be worked on and shared, whether on reddit or discord.

    Packed Bug Fixes
    
    Wiki:
    Harmonic Energy's entry in the Perks page has updated numbers to reflect the three new species.
    Governor tech's effect now shows properly in the wiki.
    Governor tech now shows the requirements of needing the Governance CRISPR and not being Anarchy.
    Carnivore trait now mentions food spoilage.
    
    Queue:
    The Asteroid Redirect ARPA project will now update its name on the ARPA -> Projects page and in the queue if the name changes.
    If there are any queued Amphitheatres/Stadiums or Apartments/Mansions during a Governor change that would cause those building names to change, those queued buildings will now have their names updated in the queue.
    Any queued Trade Posts are now removed upon adding Terrifying.
    Any queued Shrines are now removed upon removing Magnificent.
    Any queued city/space Forge Horseshoes are now removed upon removing Hooved.
    Any queued Meditation Chambers are now removed upon removing Calm.
    
    Misc:
    The Slave Market button will now update it's affordable status consistently and show an affordable timer.
    The Spy Operator task will no longer fire for Foreign Powers that are currently controlled.
    Fixed bug where Minor Traits that had not been Phaged would persist throughout resets within mtorder, automatically being unlocked on future runs.
    Mansions now say in their tooltips that they provide housing for 6 people, not just 5.
    Railway tooltip in Cataclysm now accounts for Banana Smoothie perks.
    In the Harmonic Energy perk entries, it now lists the reduction on the East and West Towers that it provides.
    Fixed some typos.
    
    Updated Pig Latin.

    For any Perks that have varying numerical effect now specify all those numerical variances in the Wiki Perks page instead of just showing the lowest number if unearned or the highest level of the effect earned. Note that the Stats -> Perks tab will still just show the perks' effects currently gained.
    EX:  Joyless Perk in the Wiki Perks page now shows "+2/4/6/8/10%" as a whole instead of just +2% or +4% or +6%, etc.

commit bb014a913ebf00ffe4626f3940d5a07e2db59fc1
Author: Beorseder <45007766+Beorseder@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Wed May 12 10:09:07 2021 -0600

    Multiple Bug Fixes
    
    Text:
    Fixed bug where Vault1 would say that it needed all 100 Soul Gems, despite Smoldering reducing the cost down to 90.
    Fixed bug where font sizes would be changed to default upon changing theme, regardless of what the font settings were.
    Fixed bug where Discharge multiplier could be seen on Copper and Iron breakdowns if a Mine was powered, yet no Miners were assigned.
    Fixed Dark Energy rounding issues in Heavy universe.
    Crafting tooltips now show a "To Empty" timer below the bonus breakdown if they have negative production and don't have 0 of the resource. A "To Full" timer is unnecessary as it would always say [Never]. Fixes #579
    Fixed some typos.
    Updated Pig Latin.
    
    Wiki:
    Updated Brute wiki tooltip and values to match the actual effects of Brute.
    Fixed bug where the Soul Gem section in the Mechanics page of the wiki could not be jumped to from the sidebar.
    Alien1 and Alien2's respective systems in the Piracy section of the wiki now use the correct system names of Alien1 Home and Alien2 Red Planet, instead of just the species names.
    Traits with values now show those values in the Traits page of the wiki.
    Increased specification that Asteroid Redirect does not contribute to Banana Smoothie nor any other mass-goal achievements in its wiki entry.
    
    Mechanics:
    Fixed bug where Gate Turrets did not actually contribute to Demon Kills, Soul Forge souls, nor Soul Gems whatsoever.
    Fixed bug where Transports and Supply routes could be manipulated in ways in which negative Supply routes could be set, allowing for potentially massive generation of nearly any resource in the game.
    Fixed bug where an infinite supply of Soul Gems could be generated by repeatedly doing Exotic Infusion and Restore Backup, gaining +1 Soul Gem from each Exotic Infusion.
    Fixed bug where Banana Smoothie would be immediately awarded in another universe at the level that its general level was at upon entering the scenario.
    If the player does not have a custom species, then the custom can no longer be selected as an alien, fixing the bug where such occurrences would cause the player to be unable to progress through Andromeda.
    Fixed bug where an attack with 0 Soldiers could be made once if the number of Soldiers alive was brought down to 0, yet the Battalion size was not 0.

    If a Boss is equally weak/resistant to all weapons, then Weak/Resist are replaced with "None" to indicate that there is no best/worse weapon.
    
    Misc:

    Tax Revolts can no longer get rid of Corrupt Soul Gem, Codex, Demonic Essence, Blood Stones, nor Artifacts.
    Fixed bug where a building with a resource cost of 0 would not be purchasable if 0 of that resource is owned and production is negative.

    Motherlode descriptions are now updated to say that achieving greatness is the requirement, not just Bioseed.
    Fixed issue in breakdown popover where a vertical line would appear to the left of the second consume column even if there was no first production column to go along with it.

    Numerable Bug Fixes
    
    Storage:
    Puchasing a Shed now instantly updates Chrysotile and Crystal caps instead of waiting for the midloop.
    Puchasing a Garage now instantly updates many resource caps instead of waiting for the midloop.
    Chrysotile now shows up in the Interstellar Warehouse tooltip and cap  is immediately added upon building one.
    
    Smoldering:
    With Smoldering, building a Rock Quarry will unlock the Civics -> Industry tab, instead of having to wait to build a Smelter to change Chrysotile Ratio in Industry.
    Fixed bug where Lumber was still a fuel option with Smoldering.
    Lumber Rituals no longer appear with Smoldering, and any pre-existing Lumber Rituals are purged with Smoldering.
    Fixed tooltip bugs with Chrysotile Ratio at 0% and 100%.
    Chrysotile now show up in the Garage tooltip during Cataclysm.
    Updated the Reclaimer, Axe, and Saw trees' Special Requirements to accomodate new Smoldering effects in the wiki.
    
    Hell:
    Fixed bug where having less than 1 Dark Energy in Evil universe would decrease Soul Gem drop rate.
    Fixed bug where Mech Lab tab wouldn't load if accessed from Mech Bay.
    Vault now has a queue max of 1.
    Fixed bug where Sphinx's description would undefined most of the time in the wiki.
    
    Wiki:
    Added Extra Requirements in the wiki for CRISPR upgrades that have them.
    Bone Tools now has the correct effects in the wiki with Smoldering.
    Added the Dark Energy Bomb's waygate2 requirement to the wiki.
    Updated Bone/Wooden Tools requirements to accomodate Demonic races in Evil universe.
    Added the missing Special Requirements that Republic and Socialist have to the wiki.
    Elusive now mentions how it affects Ambush chances and both Elusive and Chameleon now say the % they reduce chances of Ambush by.

    Sacrificial Altar can no longer sacrifice an upwards of 25000 non-existent Citizens when the default job is Unemployed. Fixes #485
    Fixed issue where building queue popovers for a building would stay after removing it from queue. Fixes #441
    Battalion now disallows attacking with a negative number of Soldiers, and will set the Battalion size to 0 if it goes below. Fixes #443
    Cataclysm reset no longer grants rapid_mutation and ancient_ruins bonuses.
    Cataclysm no longer has the power grid hidden. Fixes #491
    Outside of Cataclysm, now Craftsmen won't appear as a job role until a Foundry is gotten to unlock them.
    Fixed issue where the trait gained from Deify Ancients didn't immediately appear under listed traits, making players think they didn't get it.

commit a37b2f2e75cbf089dd39b92aa8f7e7832818176b
Author: Beorseder <45007766+Beorseder@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Sun Dec 6 00:37:20 2020 -0700

    Negative Crate/Container Handling
    
    Added handling for when the amount of free Crates/Containers goes negative. This can happen when assigning Crates/Containers earned from Arcologies, and then proceeding to turn them off Arcologies and/or lower Quantum Level to reduce the number of Crates/Containers they provide.
    When the number of free Crates/Containers goes negative, the game will start unassigning them from resources starting at the top of the list going to the bottom, until the number is no longer negative.
    It goes from top to bottom as resources on the bottom of the list commonly have fewer sources of storage other than Crates/Containers, if any, and are more valuable.

commit 09f4178bcb1034580e6460455d007f63a8655c78
Author: Beorseder <45007766+Beorseder@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Sun Dec 6 00:37:03 2020 -0700

    Assembled Bug Fixes
    
    Metal Refinery:
    Alternative string for Sappy now correctly displays on Metal Refineries when it should.
    Fixed issue where Sheet Metal could appear as a resource from getting a Metal Refinery before any Foundries were built.
    
    Vacuum Collapse:
    Vacuum Collapse no longer removes a players Corrupted bonus entirely.
    Dark Energy gained from Vacuum Collapse now properly contributes to the Dark Energy Earned stat. Current Dark Energy Earned is updated to account for any prior misalignment.
    
    Wiki:
    Both versions of Urban Planning no longer appear on the wiki, only the one that is currently applicable.
    Electricity tech on the wiki now mentions that it unlocks the Power Grid tab.
    Advanced Gun Emplacement tech on the wiki now mentions that it increases the effectiveness of Gate Turrets as well.
    Wiki explanations of how to get The Misery, Crossed the Finish Line, and Garbage Pie now all mention that Demonic Infusion resets work for earning them.
    Fixed a typo and incorrect value in a couple wiki strings.
    
    Queue:
    Queued ARPA projects now follow the same convention of designating "action" as the category it belongs to and "type" as the specific item being queued. Currently queued ARPA projects get their "action" and "type" corrected.
    Queued Sheds/Barns will now update to their Barn/Warehouse versions when the appropriate research that changes their name is purchased. Same with queued Automated/Laser Turrets updating to Laser/Plasma Turrets.
    Queued buildings and researches will now update their names upon switching languages.
    
    Misc:
    Evil races now have the Lumber Ritual hidden, as it does nothing for them. Currently assigned Lumber Rituals with Evil races get unassigned.
    Rituals now tell now say how much they're boosting something by in their tooltips.
    Plasmid, Anti-Plasmid, and Phage tooltips no longer incorrectly include the storage bonus from Harmonic Energy in their calclulation.
    Fixed issue with Shrines not applying to Adamantite from Armed Mining Ships and displaying a much larger bonus than they were providing in the Adamantite tooltip.
    Mega Factories now update the Industry page upon building them.
    Fixed issue with Containers not appearing in resource Crate/Container modals after unlocking them from non-Container Port buildings.
    Updated Pig Latin strings.

Author: Beorseder <45007766+Beorseder@users.noreply.github.com>

    Assignment Bug Fixes + Build
    
    Hell Forge:
    Building Hell Forges now updates the Scarletite Craftsman counter in the Civics tab immediately, instead of needing another update to it to see the changes.
    Powering on/off Hell Forges now also updates the Scarletite Craftsman counter.
    Powering off Hell Forges will now remove any assigned Scarletite Craftsmen that no longer have a powered Hell Forge to work in, fixing the bug where a player could power off Hell Forges and keep producing Scarletite at no detriment.
    
    Industry:
    Mining Droids, Graphene Plants, and Smelters will now unassign fuel/operating assignments if turned off, fixing the following bugs:
     - Bug where turning off Stellar Forges/Hell Forges would keep the Smelter Capacity that you have before turning them off, letting a player to produce more than they should.
     - Bugs with the color indicator for Fueled/Operating numbers breaking by having a greater number of Fueled/Operating slots than possible for the current max.
    Fixed overall bugginess with Graphene Plant fuel capacity and assignment.
    Removed extraneous code from Graphene Plant fuel assignment operators.
    
    Misc:
    Fixed bug with Wrath levels only applying to mechs when fighting the Demon Lord.

commit 2a2c57dee09384e8d72b275e54e8ce9b8ab2df2f
Author: Beorseder <45007766+Beorseder@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Tue Jul 28 06:15:45 2020 -0600

    Amassed Bug Fixes
    
    Visual Fixes:
    In Antimatter, the Ascension tech now correctly shows that it costs Anti-Plasmids instead of regular Plasmids.
    The Quarry Worker job tooltip will now state that they produce Aluminum as well as Stone, after Aluminum is unlocked.
    Lodges and Farms after Farm Houses will make the Civics tab and species resource visible, if they are not already.
    The bonus to Armed Miners from Ore Processors now correctly states that Ore Proessors give the bonus in resource tooltips, previously stating that Footholds did.
    Fixed issue where Theocracy didn't display the "Priests boost Ziggurats" effect until switching over to it.
    Plasmid, Antiplasmid, and Phage tooltips will no longer display that they are providing a storage bonus if the required CRISPR upgrades for them are not met.
    
    Wiki:
    The Planetary and Interstellar pages within the Structures category now correctly show all of the buildings in their respective regions, instead of only a few.
    The Humpback trait now explains how it also boosts Lumberjack and Mining jobs.
    Fixed the Soul Link tech effect not explaining that it also affected Gun Emplacements.
    Moved the tech effect description of the Portals tech correctly over to Fortifications.
    Fixed Slow and Hyper trait effect descriptions.
    Fixed Musical trait typo.
    Fixed NaN Food appearing with Composts in wiki.
    Old_Gods is now a condition of Ancients, instead of a requirement, so that it doesn't show up on the wiki as a requirement and confuse players as it's not a CRISPR upgrade.
    
    Misc:
    Unlocking Nanoweave through Infiltrator now reloads the craftsmen automatically, instead of needing to reload the page to see the Nanoweave craftsman.
    The number of assigned Surveyors is set to 0 after a fortress wipe, to avoid senseless death.
    Fixed issue where Antimatter Ziggurats in Cataclysm didn't boost Antiplasmid storage.
    Fixed issue where Slaves could be gained past the new cap from attacking.
    FIxed bug where building a Sawmill would multiply Lumber production by a lot until a page refresh. Fixes #399 Fixes #397
    Prior to having Transcendence, both Anthropology and Fanaticism can no longer be queued at the same time. Fixes #377

commit 4269c6c73375431c594949e8a6606a13f5a306b3
Author: Beorseder <45007766+Beorseder@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Wed May 27 05:46:18 2020 -0600

    Autodeoccupation Addition/Fix + Build
    
    Currently, when occupying Foreign Powers and then turning off buildings that provide Soldiers, the Garrison can end up with a negative amount of Soldiers. This causes numbers to jump back and forth between negative and 0, and occasionally causing the Wounded to irreversibly turn negative.
    The autodeoccupation system will automatically deoccupy a Foreign Power(s) if the Soldiers they are using would make the number of Soldiers in the Garrison turn negative.

commit 7c088b204a9c6e614714e0ecde0da1b69787e776
Author: Beorseder <45007766+Beorseder@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Wed May 27 05:44:40 2020 -0600

    Ample Bug Fixes
    
    Power:
    The power given from Windmills is no longer affected by EM Field.
    The tooltips for Windmills now display the correct amount of power given when affected by Dark Energy in Antimatter.
    Elerium Reactors no longer give double the power when active but receiving no fuel.
    
    Industry:
    Fixed bug where Smelters in the Industry tab would not show Oil as a possible fuel source immediately after unlocking Oil.
    With Kindling Kindred, Graphene Plants default to using Oil as fuel, instead of nothing.
    
    Wiki:
    Fixed issue with two versions of Fanaticism and Anthropology appearing at the same time on the wiki. Fixes #354
    The Heavyweight achievement tooltip in the wiki no longer displays Angelic as a possible genus for progression.
    
    Foreign Powers:
    Fixed issue where Federation required a page reload to appear after Annexing/Purchasing/Occupying a Foreign Power.
    Deoccupation during Unification gives back the right number of Soldiers with Federation.
    
    Typos:
    Pluralized a couple instances of 'genus'.
    Fixed 'concume' typo with the Detrivore trait.
    
    Misc:
    Blank Slate feat is no longer is impossible with the Evil trait.
    Adding/Removing Hyper and Slow now reloads the page to update the speed of the game.
    With Kindling Kindred, the galactic trade for Graphene requires 1000 Stone per route instead of 1000 Lumber.
    Fixed rounding issues when gaining Harmony Crystals.
    Fixed bug where Soft Resetting would get rid of an Ascended planet bonus.
    Fixed bug where Jump Ship costs were affected by Heavy universe and the Heavyweight perk.

commit 462877ecc83b4f14c48ae5b8c9096172ab38617a
Author: Beorseder <45007766+Beorseder@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Mon Feb 10 23:31:36 2020 -0700

    Steelen Difficulty Increase #2
    
    The requirement for completion of Steelen is now to Bioseed. This makes Steelen fit better into the other Challenge Modes, making their end-goals more evenly distributed across the game. This also makes Steelen somewhat significantly harder, as one has to consider balancing Trade Routes to have a steady source of Steel among the various other resources that are commonly Traded for during Space. A person may also likely choose to forfeit Unification, which is a commonly unpopular choice, in favor of more Steel from Combat, perhaps invoking a more varied gameplay style than during regular runs.
